Characters

Shinji Akatsu - Main character. A bookworm with a suspicious personality.
Akashi Yuuma - A person who became Shinji's friend. Soccer club. Good at English.
Sumire Uenishi - Shinji's friend who is good at mathematics.
Peresia Sero Tarinkov - A woman wearing the sacred twelve clothes.
Castelia Glenveldt - A blonde, blue-eyed girl. have special abilities.
Yoshi Yazaki - The person at the center of the Misakigaoka High School murder case


　†


Chapter 1 Encounter


“Eine Kleine Nacht Musik?”


The person who looked into my face with a startled look was Sumire Uenishi. Perhaps because the character for violet is difficult, it is often confused by teachers. Read as violet.


"Akatsu-kun, you always read books like that...Last week was Horizon?"
"Well, why do you care about that?"
This guy named Uenishi checks the title every time I buy a book. I'd like to know why they would do such a thing.


This year, I will be in my second year of high school, and while my classmates are studying for entrance exams one after another, I'm sitting on my back reading manga and novels. Studying and club activities. When I think about myself being caught up in such mundane things, I get a feeling of being boring.
“Kenishi, would you mind showing me your homework from yesterday?”
I learned from a family incident that such requests to others should always be done politely.
"Homework? What?"
"It's mathematics, what is that? What are complex numbers?"
Uenishi is a science girl at heart, and most of what she says sounds theoretical. Just as I was thinking how strange this was, a piece of homework suddenly landed on my desk.
"Have you already done that? I was just trying to make a joke..."
"Aren't complex domain problems easy? Especially with Akatsu-kun."
``I'm sorry, but I'm the type of person who just wants to do math and don't want to mess around with numbers.''
"What do you mean?"
I always think to myself, ``Come on, let's stop talking about homework.''
"No, that's fine. Thank you."
"Do you think you're just here for math?"
"Hmm, well, that's not what I mean..."
“What do you mean?”

Chapter 1 Encounter


“Eine Kleine Nacht Musik?”


The person who looked into my face with a startled look was Sumire Uenishi. Perhaps because the character for violet is difficult, it is often confused by teachers. Read as violet.


"Akatsu-kun, you always read books like that...Last week was Horizon?"
"Well, why do you care about that?"
This guy named Uenishi checks the title every time I buy a book. I'd like to know why they would do such a thing.


This year, I will be in my second year of high school, and while my classmates are studying for entrance exams one after another, I'm sitting on my back reading manga and novels. Studying and club activities. When I think about myself being caught up in such mundane things, I get a feeling of being boring.
“Kenishi, would you mind showing me your homework from yesterday?”
I learned from a family incident that such requests to others should always be done politely.
"Homework? What?"
"It's mathematics, what is that? What are complex numbers?"
Uenishi is a science girl at heart, and most of what she says sounds theoretical. Just as I was thinking how strange this was, a piece of homework suddenly landed on my desk.
"Have you already done that? I was just trying to make a joke..."
"Aren't complex domain problems easy? Especially with Akatsu-kun."
``I'm sorry, but I'm the type of person who just wants to do math and don't want to mess around with numbers.''
"What do you mean?"
I always think to myself, ``Come on, let's stop talking about homework.''
"No, that's fine. Thank you."
"Do you think you're just here for math?"
"Hmm, well, that's not what I mean..."
“What do you mean?”

He really is...a guy... Well, it's better not to provoke your true feelings too much. Both for me and for Uenishi.
"There's no explanation. That's just the way it is. Not in my house."


The pain was so great that my back muscles relaxed.
“Hey.”
Uenishi didn't say that to my face, but he was exclaiming as he looked at the train running in the distance. That's what it sounded like to me.


I saw a movie recently. It's also an American comic about zombies. This may sound like very common content, but I'm totally in love with it. There are many times when I think that something that someone is addicted to is not worth it, but I feel like I can return it by thinking that it was a mistake after all and turning into a stupid sage.
"It's really well made. Internet video sites already have this good quality."
I reveal that I live in a dormitory, but the person who just spoke was not me, but a third-year high school boy named Akashi. He's on the soccer club, and personally, he's the most grumpy guy.
"Why do you care? You're lucky that the picture quality is good."
"Akazu, don't you understand? When it comes to videos, the quality of the video is what counts. No matter how great the video is, it won't matter if the quality of the video is FUCKING."
"You have a point. It's true that something that can be removed cannot be removed."
The school's dormitory is divided into a boys' dormitory and a girls' dormitory, with the boys' dormitory located beyond the gymnasium, and the girls' dormitory located a little further away from the school grounds. There were dozens of students in the boys' dormitory, including me, and Akashi Yuuma happened to be one of them who shared a room with me.
"Hey, Akashi, aren't you interested in foreign countries?"
"Foreign country? For example?"
“America or England?”
"Why?"
Akashi leaned heavily against the back of the chair.
“Do you know about Test Land?”
“What is that?”
``It's an American drama novel, and I've been hooked on it lately.''
"Ah, but you're like a bookworm, so you'll probably get hooked on anything."
"No, this is special. I don't care about anyone else."
"Hey, it seems like you can say it quite clearly. Well, I guess I'll lend you a little bit."
"Okay."

He really is...a guy... Well, it's better not to provoke your true feelings too much. Both for me and for Uenishi.
"There's no explanation. That's just the way it is. Not in my house."


The pain was so great that my back muscles relaxed.
“Hey.”
Uenishi didn't say that to my face, but he was exclaiming as he looked at the train running in the distance. That's what it sounded like to me.

"No, this is special. I don't care about anyone else."
"Hey, it seems like you can say it quite clearly. Well, I guess I'll lend you a little bit."
"Okay."

I talk to Akashi like this every time. Talking with Akashi gets more exciting when you talk without really thinking. The reason is a mystery.
“Tsukasa, it seems that the guy from Nishinomiya has come on a trip?”
Akashi started talking about a new topic while trying to pick up the book next to me.
"Nishinomiya?"
"That's right, Akari Nishimiya."
"Where have you been traveling?"
"Hmm, I don't know where that is. I think it was probably Europe."
"Hmm, so? What happened to that?"
"They were handing out some kind of souvenirs yesterday, right? I just saw them."
"Seriously, does anyone in this school have that kind of money?"
"Money? What do you mean?"
Akashi had the Hatena mark pressed on his nose.
“Look, there was someone at this school who went overseas.”
"Hmm...that's true...but if you want to go, you can go, right?"
"Really?"
Akashi was combing his short hair with his hand as he stared at the book he took from me.

Night as usual-
School as usual-


And as usual-


"Oh, how boring."
"Hmm."
Akashi was still in the room.
"Hey, weren't you going to eat with those guys?"
"It's such a hassle..."
"Really?"
As you can see, Akashi is addicted to my book. Rather than being addicted to it, it's more like I'm so absorbed in it that I don't care about what's going on around me anymore.
“Aren’t you the one who won’t be invited by Uenishi?”
Suddenly, he tried to turn back on me.
"Huh? From Uenishi? Why do I have to be invited by such a mysterious girl?"
"My name is Fushigi-chan."
Akashi was still reading his book while sighing.
"Well, it's time to go to sleep now, so good night Mingo."
I have a habit of adding humorous endings to words to muddy the air when I don't understand something. However, Akashi, who was supposed to receive it, didn't pay attention to such a greeting.

「カステリアだ…入るぞ？」
カステリアは男の家を訪ねた。
"What are you? I thought you were some little girl."


"Little girl? Where? Is this your favorite joke again?"


「はいはい、すいません」


Castelia complained to Sebastores, who was across from him.
"Hey, this! The coffee is too bitter!"
"Is your coffee bitter? You're a little girl after all, aren't you?"
Sebastres immediately provokes Castelia.カステリアは、見た目が完全にセバストレスのいうそれで、金髪ロングに黄色い瞳を持つ、いわゆる合法ロリータお姫様と化していた。
"If you're not a little girl, hurry up and make me a cup of coffee again!"
"Huh? That's the one I made for myself... If you don't like it that much, go back to Felherd."
“No, who would go back to such a shady place!”
「じゃあすこし黙ってろアホ！」
The conversation between the two began as if they were having a quarrel.セバストレスは赤い髪を持ち、つんつんヘアーで蒼い瞳、そしてジャラジャラとしたアクセサリー多数に腕には豪快な刺繍が施されていた。 As for his attire, he wears a tailcoat, which is rare in this world.一方カステリアは、燕尾服ではないが、真っ黒のワンピースを着ていて、なんとはだしで出歩いているらしい。
カステリアは、セバストレス邸の３メートル級ソファーに寝っ転がりながらポケットに手を突っ込んで思いにふけっていた。
"Hey, what do you want? I haven't asked you that yet."
「用なんて気にするの？あほ？」
"I understand that you're picking on me, but I'm being generous. Why did you come here?"
"Isn't that what you do in your free time? You really are an idiot."
Sebastress was furious at Castelia's words.
"Castelia, I'll teach you what the Buddha's face is!"
Castelia felt Sebastress attack and immediately covered herself with both arms. The two of them held each other's hands as Castelia fell into the sofa.
"Wow, Sebas is surprisingly powerful...I'm impressed."
「そりゃどうも、カステリア嬢‼」
Sebastores tried to crush Castelia.

"Yo!!"


Boom!


Then, the wine bottle was released with great force and flew towards Castelia, following the laws of physics. I thought it was going to hit Castelia, but instead of dodging, it landed in Castelia's right hand.

Paci!


"Thank you"
Castelia soon poured wine down his throat.

“Kurulu is a nice person though.”
While drinking from a bottle of wine, he occasionally stops drinking and replies to Sebastian.
"Sebastres is a little tough on me. Do you know what I mean?"

The conversation between the two began as if they were having a quarrel. Sebastress has red hair, spiky hair, blue eyes, and many jangly accessories and gorgeous embroidery on her arms. As for his attire, he wears a tailcoat, which is rare in this world. Castelia, on the other hand, is not wearing a tailcoat, but is wearing a pitch black dress, and apparently goes out barefoot.
Castelia was lying on a three-meter sofa in the Sebastianre residence, hands in his pockets, lost in thought.

"Do you care about business? Aho?"

"Isn't that what you do in your free time? You really are an idiot."
Sebastress was furious at Castelia's words.
"Castelia, I'll teach you what the Buddha's face is!"
Castelia felt Sebastress attack and immediately covered herself with both arms. The two of them held each other's hands as Castelia fell into the sofa.
"Wow, Sebas is surprisingly powerful...I'm impressed."

Sebastores tried to crush Castelia.

"It's sweet."
Then, Castelia quickly pushed Sebastianre's arms to the left and instantly escaped from the sofa. It happened so suddenly that Sebastress fell face down on the sofa as if he had been caught off guard.
“Fugu!?”
"Please just stay asleep! Sebastress!"
Castelia tried to elbow Sebastian from above. However, Sebastress also resisted and fended off the attack. Sebastores managed to escape Castelia's counterattack.
“Huh, you’re doing a surprisingly good job, Castelia.”
Sebastress picked up the wine bottle next to him and played with it.
"Your house is bigger than yours, so it's easy to do. But, what will happen if we mess with Castelia-sama? Maybe even his proud mansion will become his lungs?"

Boom!

"I'm not in this class, but do you know Mr. Yazaki, a third year student?"
When the topic changed, Uenishi's expression became cloudy, as if dark clouds were gathering.
"Yazaki? I don't know."
Uenishi looked even more suspicious than usual.
"His name is Yazaki Zen-kun, but there seems to be some bad rumors around the school."
"Bad rumors? What is that?" It sounded like a joke, but I was a little intrigued. Soon, Sumire opened her mouth unilaterally, contrary to my hesitation.
"Yeah, it looks like some kind of murder happened..."
It was just a whisper, but it wasn't anything serious.
"Murder? Hey hey...what's that?"
What was that really? I've never heard of such bad reviews at this school. Whether that was true or not could only be read from Uenishi's expression at this point. And if it really turns out to be murder... There's no point in thinking about it, but in any case, I feel like a dark shadow has fallen into my backfield regarding my current living environment as a whole.
"Yeah, so now? It's been around for the last week or so, and the third graders have been talking about it all..."
"What's that...since last week? Is this the first time you've heard about it?"
"Maybe it's because it has nothing to do with us second year students. Only people like me who have the information can say things like this..."
“Who did you hear that from?”

"I heard it from my sister..."
Uenishi has an older sister. I knew this too. However, even though such information came from my sister... "Didn't you think what your sister was saying was wrong?"
"I don't think so...I mean, Shiori is the most honest person in the family, right?"
"Well, it's probably true... So, you're telling me to be wary of that guy?"
"It's probably fine out of ten, but just in case."
Unlike usual, I felt that Uenishi's words had no power.


"I guess the teachers at school won't tell us things like that... It certainly seems like they can treat us like strangers..."
Even though I knew it had nothing to do with it, I didn't know how much it would infiltrate me. According to information from Uenishi, one person was killed. I don't seem to know if he was connected to this school or not.
"Kenishi, have any incidents like this ever happened since you started at this school? I mean, you say it's a murder, but has the dead victim been found?"
"They've found it. It looks like there's definitely one dead person... Someone even released a photo... Also, something like this has never happened before. In my opinion..."
"Are you making the photos public? Does that mean you're taking photos of dead people directly with your smartphone and distributing them?"
"It seems that the photo was on a restricted network off-campus...This is also information from Shiori..."
"Hmm, he's a surprisingly dangerous guy...Zen Yazaki."
Apparently, Yazaki himself does not come to this school. Well, if things go sour, I can't avoid being sent to prison...


It can be quite difficult to carry out daily routines. This time, the school gave me homework, and as expected, mathematics was the worst part.
"Shit...I don't understand."
"Hey, you're a science student, right?"
Akashi was eating a cup of ramen behind him and encouraging him.
"Akashi...you..."
"Oh yeah, that guy called Shintaro Miyazaki was calling you, right? For the past year."
"Miyazaki...what? Is this some kind of invitation?"
"Come on."


Anyway, I decided to meet with Miyazaki at a later date.

But that's not the case now. It's mathematics. It would be appropriate to ask Uenishi here... If Uenishi is not there...


"Sorry."
I invaded the first grade classroom for the first time in a while.
“Does Miyazaki exist?”
"Yes"
That's what was in front of me.
"Shintaro Miyazaki-kun? I'm Akatsu, but...do you have any requirements?"
"Akatsu-senpai! Hello...! Yo, I have a requirement!"
Judging from the awkwardness, I once again thought that he was a first year student.
"What?"
“This is it!”
What he handed me was a mysterious document. It was about 3 pages long, but it was written in English.
“What is this?”
"I found it on the side of the road... and when I opened it, there was a note written for Mr. Shinji Akatsu..."
Miyazaki looks worried for some reason. Are you concerned about my mood?
"Hey, I appreciate your courage... Well, thank you. And I have a favor to ask of you as well."


"Huh? Is this your math homework?"
As soon as he put the letter away, Miyazaki brightened up, as if he had turned over his hand.
"Well, I'm sure you're good at math, right? My classmate told me so."
“I’m sure I’m good at it, but…”
That's why I showed it to you.
"This...isn't mathematics, senpai...analytical mechanics...physics."
"Huh?"
When I looked closely, I saw Physics 3 written in large letters on it. I couldn't even close my open mouth.


However, even difficult physics homework was easily solved by Miyazaki. What a guy. At that moment, I felt like this was my second Kamishi. I wanted to tell him that he should join my community right away, but since the only requirement was to hand over a document, I lost that desire.

For some reason, they hang out near the entrance every day. Among is a popular boy band these days. And Aeros is an abbreviation for A L The Eros, which is a girl group. Both of them boasted the top sales in Japan, and these two forces divided the world's music fans into two.
After listening to this everyday conversation, I made my way to the second floor where the classroom was located.


"Good morning. Akatsu-kun."

"I'm sorry. Castelia... I don't know what you have. That's what you really want, but please back off from here..."
For some reason, the feeling of helplessness has shifted even to me. Even though I was the one who was being thrown around a lot.
Castelia left the Uchida family. I went back to school so that I could follow.


"I'm here. Get off."


By the time I heard Castelia's voice, it was already 4:30. The school was right in front of me.


"I think I'm going home now."


You suddenly start saying that, so where are you going? That's what I thought, but it was probably the guy who said 5 hours or something.
“Is there a time limit or something?”
I happened to take a look.
"Ah. I have a limited amount of time to work here. I think I told you this when I met you."
Ah, I think I definitely heard that.


“What happens if it passes?”


"...It may be hard to believe, but it will physically disappear. From this place."


"Huh? Will it disappear?"
I couldn't hide my surprise. I had already forgotten where reality was.
"Well, I think I can go home with plenty of time this time."
Castelia's expression showed a hint of regret. I wonder if he is worried about Uchida after all.
"Maybe I'll come here again. I'm sure it will be for the same reason then."
Has his cool demeanor remained the same? Well, let's just say I don't know much about it.


Castelia said, ``Don't leave me alone,'' and she put her hand on her chest right in front of me and disappeared.
Although it only happened for a moment, I couldn't help but believe my eyes.
"It disappeared...really..."


It's too meaningless. Castelia… Grenwerth…. What on earth is he...?


It was like I was wandering between fantasy and reality for four hours.


Chapter 3 After the Storm


Even after Castelia disappeared, I still couldn't escape from the memories of that fantastic experience. However, that delusion collapsed in an unexpected way.


"It's cold!"


Now that I think about it, he did something strange to me and stole my sleep. Only now did I become aware of the current situation due to the abnormally low temperature around me.


*

I make some hand gestures and hope that Castelia will understand.
"Of course, but that has a slightly different meaning from predicting the future. It's more uncertain than predicting the future."

What Castelia says goes beyond common sense. Isn't it extremely difficult for me to understand what she wants me to understand now? I don't even have time to think about it.
"Ah, in contrast to that uncertain factor, killing Uchida could be more certain. That's just what I did."
“…Did you try to kill Uchida with something like that?”
All I could think of were three words: Uchida, it couldn't be helped, and I could kill him.
"So I told you, what do you think will happen if he doesn't die? I'm only human. Let me make my quota a little easier."


I still didn't understand the meaning. When it comes to killing people, there are three words: quota. It may be true that he is an assassin, but he doesn't hesitate to involve others in order to save people. This doesn't make sense. If he was being serious, there's no way this guy would be wandering around dressed like this.
"It seems like the quota you're talking about is quite selfish. What's the reason you're so particular about it?"


I thought this was a question that got to the core of something.


"I'm sorry, Akatsu, but there's nothing more I can tell you. I have my own position."
There was a sudden break in the conversation. What does position mean? It became more and more incomprehensible.
"Then I won't ask you any more. In return, I have a wish as well."
I came up with the idea to replace it.
"...?"
"Don't kill Uchida. Or rather, I hope you don't kill him."
Whatever the reason, it would be wrong to kill Uchida. It was unwavering.
“…”
Castelia's face becomes dull. It was really a mystery what kind of existence Uchida was to this guy. Well, that's good for now. Right now, I was looking for a way to resolve this situation peacefully.


"...I can't help it. Let's stand down here."
After thinking about it, Castelia said yes.

3rd year class A.
Akashi always talks about his junior named Akatsu. Yet, strangely, people gather around him. Nishimiya slammed the book he was reading and walked towards his usual female companions with a look of shame on his face.
"Akari? You're a little busy right now, aren't you?"
I called out to Sato and Kuriki from Class C, who had gone on an overseas trip together, but they were in the middle of studying for entrance exams. Nishimiya's grades were fair to good, but the person behind him, Shuji, wasn't doing so well. Kuriki knows this.
"Shuuji? Are you okay with your studies? You won't get into a good university if you hang out with Akari, right?"
　We receive simple and direct feedback. Although she seemed hateful to Akari and the others, she was an excellent high school girl who ranked third in her class. With Shuji's grades, you can't really make fun of this guy.
"Nishinomiya, aren't you really into Akashi after all? It seems like that from the look on his face, but...it's boring."
Kuriki also provokes Nishimiya. Even when asked why Nishimiya went abroad with Kuriki, the most plausible reason is that he was part of the story. Originally, this was the kind of relationship he had with Kuriki.
 "Kokuhaku? When did I say that?"
Nishimiya was a little upset. Sato was with Kuriki, but perhaps because of his shy nature, he didn't get involved.
Akashi happened to be passing by just then. "Ah, Akashi!" When Nishimiya put his hand on him, Akashi stopped and turned around. Kuriki put his hand over his mouth and opened his eyes, saying, "Huh?"
"Akashi, there's something I want to ask you."
Nishimiya approached Akashi and started asking questions. Kuriki can't seem to close his mouth at the sudden development.
"What?" Akashi replied with a calm expression.

Shuji calls Nishimiya in a rather loud voice. In response, Nishimiya smiled and replied, "Yeah?" It seems that Shuji's question was not heard. Shuji starts saying the same thing again, saying that the book is interesting. This is a class with a popular person named Akashi.

"Akashi, there's something I want to ask you."
Nishimiya approached Akashi and started asking questions. Kuriki can't seem to close his mouth at the sudden development.
"What?" Akashi replied with a calm expression.

"I hear you're familiar with the incidents that have been happening lately, but I'm not that well-informed, so there are a lot of things I don't understand. So, there's something I'd like you to tell me."
Nishimiya started talking to Akashi about the Yazaki incident. Akashi looked around a bit, then led the group to the back of the women's restroom with Kuriki in tow.
“You guys, don’t get too involved in what I say, okay?”
What about Kuriki, Sato, and Shuji who don't know anything? With that expression on his face, he followed Nishimiya aimlessly.
"So? What are you talking about in detail?" Akashi said with narrowed eyes, and Nishimiya asked momentarily, "Are the rumors about dead bodies true?"
Even though they were in the same grade, there were people like Nishinomiya and the others who were hidden behind dark topics.
However, Akashi's behavior attracted them, as if inviting them into a gravitational field.
"Rumors about a dead body? Do you mean details about the dead body?"
"Well, I guess so. Where was it found? Who is it?"
Nishimiya crossed his arms.
"It seems that it was found in a warehouse. Her name is Mari Yui. She is an alumnus of Misakigaoka and graduated from here two years ago. And, most likely, the body was found about a week ago from now."
Sato expresses new anxiety about this.
"Ah, what do you mean by a corpse...?"
The content was shocking for those hearing it for the first time.
“Ah, you don’t know Sato?”
Nishimiya turns around and looks at Sato.
"Mr. Nishimiya? Just because you're worried about your future path, how often do you play horror suspense with your boyfriend?" Kuriki said as usual. Nishimiya was impressed, thinking that he could make a fool of himself in this situation with Akashi.
"Aren't you interested, Kuriki?"
Akashi asked Kuriki, ``Are you not interested in me?'' Kuriki flinched for a moment, but instantly regained his senses and said, ``It's not like I don't have a problem, so I'll ask you.''
he replied. Akashi thought he saw something hot and flickering in Kuriki's eyes, like a flame. However, he later realized that this was not a discovery that would lead him to the truth.

Akashi's story skipped in and out of places, and it was troublesome for the listener as well. The girls were forced to talk to each other for several minutes, but Nishimiya was the only one who was able to get into the important details.
``That's what I mean.'' By the time Akashi confidently finished the conversation, Kuriki's face had become visibly irritated.


"It's all the same. Kuriki."
After Kuriki left, Akashi muttered to himself. Kuriki got fed up with Akashi's uninteresting story and returned to the classroom with Sato.
Shuji and Nishinomiya remain with Akashi.
"Akashi, are you facing such an incident alone?"
"No, I just want to help investigate the truth of this incident."
Sakaguchi's face from the other day appeared in Akashi's mind.
"No, no matter what you think, it's not true..."
Nishimiya makes a face that says he's thinking about it using common sense, but Akashi confidently replies:
"You know Akatsu, right? He was surprisingly cooperative."
"Akatsu? 2nd year?"
"Ah, it looks like he's having a lot of trouble too."
Nishimiya nodded with a hmm expression on his face.
"Shuji? Do you know Shiori's phone number?"
Nishimiya suddenly asked Shuji for Shiori Uenishi's phone number. Shuji sheepishly replied that he understood. Shiori Uenishi hasn't been to school lately.
Akashi thought this was a separate matter and left the place. However, what Nishimiya was trying to convey to Shuji on the phone was exactly his cooperation.

Alone and stunned, Akatsu suddenly picks up the phone to tell Akashi that he will be gathering at the Uenishi family.
"Akashi?"
"Akatsu, what's wrong?"
"Can you come to Kamishi's house at 7 o'clock today? Kamishi... Shiori?"
"Why?"
"Well, that's fine."
At this time, Akashi had already heard about Akatsu's series of experiences, and predicted that it was probably connected.
"Okay. See you then."

I asked a strange question.
"What? How do you know?"
Nishimiya didn't know Akatsu's face, so he thought he was a complete outsider.

In fact, the most heretical person here is Akatsu.

Uenishi recognized Nishimiya's face, so I don't know how it happened, but it's amazing. That was the reaction.

Akashi has arrived.

Akatsu called out to everyone.

Nishinomiya looked worried.
"It's true."
Akashi followed.

Add detailed explanation. Shuji just listened silently.

"Huh?"
Akatsu reacts as if he was caught off guard.

“Notorious reputation?”
Sumire interjected.
"Yes, that person has a boyfriend...he seems older, but...he doesn't belong to this school...he doesn't seem to know who he is."
"What...?"
Nishinomiya and Akatsu overlapped again. Noticing this, they both looked at each other.
"I don't even know who he is..."
Sumire muttered.


"Then, that boyfriend disappeared somewhere along with Yui Mari... Then, last week, she was found dead in a warehouse..."
Shiori looks down.
“Is Yazaki Zen…unrelated after all?”
When Akatsu asked, Shiori replied that she didn't know.
"But I don't think Zen Yazaki is unrelated... Because... he has a friend named Akemi Nishino."
He opens his mouth and speaks again.
“Akemi Nishino?”
"Yes, she's in the same third year as me, and she's not going to school right now..."
Every year, there was a large number of third-year students refusing to attend school.
“So… what happened?”
Akashi asked, crossing his arms.
"I heard that Akemi Nishino's sister was a friend of Yui Mari...and they were also close friends."
Akatsu's eyes widen involuntarily.
"So...Nishino is quite the key person...?" Shiori nods. This is probably the closest answer to the truth.
"Then why haven't you done that until now?"
A week is even shorter. Besides, Shiori hadn't been to school since then, so there was no way she would have the courage to attack the Nishino family alone.

"Damn...if only I had thought about it a little longer..."
Immediately, Uchida opened his mouth.
"Haa, haa, I won't let the ambulance get here..."
"What are you talking about...!" If you think about it, Akatsu is actually a high school student. And so are all the people who have said this.
“Well, I’ll give you one hint… This is the best trick I know…!”
Uchida slowly opened his mouth.
“What?”
Akatsu is upset.
"Mari Yui's lover is... Miyashita... That's all I know. I..."
He muttered as if he had given up on something.

Akatsu firmly suppresses Uchida. However, Akatsu himself was convinced that this would not last long. However, in this situation, it seems like Akashi is the only one he can rely on, but he's holding back his eyes and can't do anything about it. Nishinomiya is doing something else.
“Uchida, I won’t ask you to do anything unreasonable… Please be quiet… I respect your opinion…!”
I desperately tried to persuade him to settle the situation.
However, Uchida's power was stronger than he expected.
"Wow!"
Akatsu was pushed down. Uchida, now free, approaches Akashi. Shiori and Sumire were there.
“It’s dangerous!”
Akatsu shouted.
At that moment, Shiori suddenly recognized Uchida and kicked him with all her might.
Uchida's posture collapsed, and Akatsu rushed in towards him.
"Thank you!"
I looked at Shiori's face. Lock it again and prevent it from moving.
"Damn..."
“Why are you acting so violently? Is this revenge for what happened the other day?”
When Akatsu asked, Uchida looked away. Apparently so.
"I feel sorry for Castelia. I'm serious about this. But this is different. Please, please be quiet!"
"Why are you guys trying to find out so much? You should realize that I didn't have anything as of yesterday!"

I wondered what I should have done. But there's no point in worrying about it. It has passed. It was Shiori who had suggested going to the Uchida family in the first place, but it was no one's fault that she had given permission to do so. However, it would be wrong to blame Shiori. This is everyone's responsibility. Naturally, that included Akashi and Shuji, who had decided to go. However, I still didn't understand this. this is….
And it's not over yet. The spark is still smoldering. I could have pulled it at any time, but I didn't. And I couldn't back down. If Akashi and his friends give up on uncovering the truth at this point, they won't be able to stand up.
What is this, a suspenseful game? What is a trip? When I come face to face with reality like this, I lose my footing. It seems like that...

"Faedev? I don't know... that kind of guy."
I'm impressed by how the conversation takes place in a completely different world.
"I-I'm sorry..."
Apparently, etiquette and etiquette are common. Since I haven't heard anything from Castelia, I feel like I'm surviving in a world that doesn't make any sense. However, intuitively, it feels like something will work out.


They reached the village meeting hall. The number of people will also increase significantly.
When I opened the door and entered, there was an audience, and beyond that was a person playing music. As I was walking through the audience, a short Castelia appeared from the other side as well.
“Did you guess anything?”
It's so noisy around me that I can't hear it. Castelia gestured with his finger for them to come outside. I have no choice but to go outside.
“…Did you find anything?”
"Nothing"
The same seems to be true of Castelia.
"This village looks a lot like our world...maybe."
I didn't think that would happen. I couldn't believe that this world and my world aren't two different worlds...
"At least it's a different world."
“…I see.”
I'm gradually getting used to Castelia.
"What are we going to do now? Is there a Fadeev in this village?"
"I don't know. From what I see, there aren't too many people who have heard of it."
Castelia looked a little dull.
Then, three young men came there. He looked about 20 years old.
"Hey, there's someone who won't watch."
One of them looked at Castelia and declared. I thought it would be noticeable if there was a guy with blond hair wearing a black coat and a guy wearing comical clothes that looked like modern people, but that didn't seem to be the cause.


"What, it's been a while since I've seen you, woman..."

As I was saying this, I looked around the village and sure enough, there was no one child or woman there.
"Seriously...?"
Apparently, this world was indeed a different world.
Castelia's face did not change at all in response to this shocking fact. Indeed, it is impossible to imagine how much incomprehension this person who does not understand the meaning must have experienced.
"Castelia? W-what should we do?"
Whisper secretly. Apparently, Castelia's existence is becoming a concern. On the other hand, the men just stare at them without trying to make a fuss.
"I'm leaving here...from this village."
Castelia muttered softly.
“Are you leaving?”
This village was certainly a bit abnormal. I stood up without saying anything, and one of the three men spoke again.
"The blonde over there. Wait a minute. Are you from the Shoshi army?"
He seems to be slightly wary. Castelia shakes her head as if she knows something.

"Is this the wall?"
I reached the wall. It was a very big wall. The height is about 15 meters. I don't know why there is a need to erect such a wall.
As Castelia approached, a woman at the checkpoint came out. It's quite heavily armored.
I quickly put on my hood.
"Can we go inside?"
Castelia asks.
"Okay, what about the one in the back?"
“…I’m with you.”
I'm trying to peek inside a little. I was worried about the future, wondering if it would be that bad. At worst, only Castelia could enter.
"...Well, that's fine. Go inside."
It seems okay, but it's not okay at all. That has too many uncertainties.
When the gate opened, I could see what was inside, but it was no different from the village from earlier. Speaking of differences, I could see something like a tower in the distance in front of me. Perhaps that is the festival venue?
Castelia immediately started collecting information about the festival. Thinking back on it now, I realized that it was a miracle that we were able to meet again after splitting into two groups. This takes courage.
"Hey, Castelia, you're surprisingly amazing..."
It was surprisingly unnecessary.
"If you do something here, you'll be in trouble...and it'll be a lot of trouble...just follow me."
It was dangerous to act alone. That could be easily deduced from the previous scene.


Castelia gradually made her way towards the tower.
"I heard that there's a huge festival going on around here..."
Ask a woman. The woman dressed like a dancer finally mentioned the festival.
“Are you talking about the Balbal ritual?”
“Balbal ritual?”
Castelia was unusually upset.
"Why don't you know? Isn't it a famous ceremony hosted by Mr. Delonde?"

However, if there was a village of that size in there, I had a feeling that a big festival would definitely be held there.

Just to be safe, I swapped my jacket for the hooded coat Castelia was wearing to prepare for the world that lay ahead.


*


"Is this the wall?"
I reached the wall. It was a very big wall. The height is about 15 meters. I don't know why there is a need to erect such a wall.
As Castelia approached, a woman at the checkpoint came out. It's quite heavily armored.
I quickly put on my hood.
"Can we go inside?"
Castelia asks.
"Okay, what about the one in the back?"
“…I’m with you.”
I'm trying to peek inside a little. I was worried about the future, wondering if it would be that bad. At worst, only Castelia could enter.
"...Well, that's fine. Go inside."
It seems okay, but it's not okay at all. That has too many uncertainties.
When the gate opened, I could see what was inside, but it was no different from the village from earlier. Speaking of differences, I could see something like a tower in the distance in front of me. Perhaps that is the festival venue?
Castelia immediately started collecting information about the festival. Thinking back on it now, I realized that it was a miracle that we were able to meet again after splitting into two groups. This takes courage.
"Hey, Castelia, you're surprisingly amazing..."
It was surprisingly unnecessary.
"If you do something here, you'll be in trouble...and it'll be a lot of trouble...just follow me."
It was dangerous to act alone. That could be easily deduced from the previous scene.


Castelia gradually made her way towards the tower.
"I heard that there's a huge festival going on around here..."
Ask a woman. The woman dressed like a dancer finally mentioned the festival.
“Are you talking about the Balbal ritual?”
“Balbal ritual?”
Castelia was unusually upset.
"Why don't you know? Isn't it a famous ceremony hosted by Mr. Delonde?"

It's a completely global term.
“Is Mr. Delonde the ruler of this town?”
Castelia asks.
"Deronde-sama is a god. A god who guides us to peace... unlike the devil..."
I don't understand the meaning of the devil or God at all.
"I see, then where is that god?"
Castelia asks relentlessly.
"I don't know about that...but isn't it near that tower?"
I thought it was rare to be able to specify the coordinates of a religious object, but I found out that there are many things in that tower.


*


Castelia walked even faster.
"Hey! Fast! Fast!"
“…Tch, you don’t have enough strength!”
"I-I'm sorry..."
“Shut up and follow me.”
There was no mention of my feet.
There was a straight line all the way to the tower, and the roads were laid out like a grid. All the women around me started looking at me. I wonder if he's reacting to the presence of a tall person he's never seen before. I silently followed Castelia. Castelia continues to move forward.


Before I knew it, the entrance gate seemed so far away.
"Oi oi, it went in quite well..."
Although I thought so, it felt like there were still many kilometers to go until I reached my destination, the tower. So far, my presence has not been discovered. However, there is no guarantee that the requirements will be able to be fulfilled without any problems. In fact, the situation is approaching the worst. There was not even a single man, let alone Fadeev.
"Hey! Castelia! Castelia!"
I call out in a hoarse voice. Castelia, who was walking in front of me, noticed this and turned around, wondering what was going on. He looks at me like that.
“Isn’t there a plan?”
“Scheme?”
"After we get to that tower. What do we do from there?"
"...Anyway, just follow me for now. If it becomes a problem, I'll deal with it."
It seems like it's a matter of leaving things to the occasion. Reluctantly, I turned forward and headed towards the tower again.


*


I arrived at the tower without any particular trouble. Apparently, looking at the signboards along the way, the name of this tower is Doggy Tower. According to the story of the woman from earlier, it seems that there is a god or something around here.
“Fah, is Fadeev around here?”
I'll ask Castelia.

I arrived at the tower without any particular trouble. Apparently, looking at the signboards along the way, the name of this tower is Doggy Tower. According to the story of the woman from earlier, it seems that there is a god or something around here.
“Fah, is Fadeev around here?”
I'll ask Castelia.

"I don't know...but let's take a guess."
With that said, Castelia stopped on the path he had come and started walking down a side street. Castelia found an alley and guided me there.
"It'll be fine here."
There are many high-rise buildings in this area. Therefore, the alley was the perfect place to hide, as no one would interfere. I take off the hood of the coat I was wearing until now.


"Ah, I'm tired. This isn't a joke at all..."
"...I'm sorry, I didn't expect to have a quota in a world like this."
Castelia looks apologetic. I didn't have the courage to be angry with this guy anymore.
"What are we going to do for now? Fadeev's bastard isn't here, right?"
"Well, I'm also curious about the Balbal ritual. I'm sure that's what the huge festival described here is all about..."
Castelia is uncharacteristically calm.
“Then what do you plan to do?”
"...I'll leave Fadeev behind for now...I want to find out the details of Balbal's ritual..."
